they are checked against the printed editions before quoting.

     ùmantÃ.
     Yo saccikaÂÂho paramaÂÂho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaÂÂhaparamaÂÂhenÃti?
     Na h' evaæ vattabbe.
     ùjÃnÃhi niggahaæ: ha¤ci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaÂÂhaparamaÂÂhena, tena vata re vattabbe "Yo saccikaÂÂho paramaÂÂho tato so puggalo uppalabbhati saccikaÂÂhaparamaÂÂhenÃti."
